         <div class="art-post-body">
          <div class="art-post-inner art-article">
           <h2 class="art-postheader">
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96904" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to A2 Supplies: Micro boom sticks &amp; tactical grab bags">
             A2 Supplies: Micro boom sticks &amp; tactical grab bags
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">
            June 23rd, 2018 | Author:
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">
             News Fairy
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="art-postcontent">
            <!-- article-content -->
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.a2supplies.co.uk/" target="_blank">
              <img align="right" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/saved_resource2.png?resize=200%2C38" style="float: right; margin: 3px; display: inline"/>
             </a>
             Here is all the latest news from
             <a href="http://www.a2supplies.co.uk/" target="_blank">
              A2 Supplies
             </a>
             :
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Micro Boom Sticks!
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               New from CYMA
              </strong>
              is the
              <strong>
               CM357 Short Shotgun!
              </strong>
              This
              <strong>
               compact Pump-Action Tri-Shot
              </strong>
              shotgun
              <strong>
               based around their 870
              </strong>
              series of shotguns. The CM357 is a
              <strong>
               light
              </strong>
              but also
              <strong>
               robust
              </strong>
              shotgun, featuring a
              <strong>
               mostly polymer construction
              </strong>
              with some
              <strong>
               metal parts.
              </strong>
              It features a
              <strong>
               comfortable goose-neck style grip
              </strong>
              in the rear with a
              <strong>
               QD sling mount
              </strong>
              allowing you to
              <strong>
               sling it as a backup weapon
              </strong>
              easily. Alongside this the
              <strong>
               top of the weapon is railed
              </strong>
              for the addition of
              <strong>
               optics,
              </strong>
              and the gun also comes with a
              <strong>
               side mounted shell saddle
              </strong>
              to keep up to
              <strong>
               4 spare shells
              </strong>
              on the gun itself! If you’ve been looking for a
              <strong>
               short
              </strong>
              but also
              <strong>
               tactical shotgun,
              </strong>
              then CYMA has the answer!
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Sawn-off-image-1.jpg" target="_blank">
               <img alt="Sawn off image 1" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="99" src="https://i0.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Sawn-off-image-1_thumb.jpg?resize=104%2C99" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="Sawn off image 1" width="104"/>
              </a>
              <a href="https://i1.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Sawn-off-image-2.jpg" target="_blank">
               <img alt="Sawn off image 2" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="104" src="https://i0.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Sawn-off-image-2_thumb.jpg?resize=104%2C104" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="Sawn off image 2" width="104"/>
              </a>
              <a href="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Sawn-off-image-3.jpg" target="_blank">
               <img alt="Sawn off image 3" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="104" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Sawn-off-image-3_thumb.jpg?resize=104%2C104" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="Sawn off image 3" width="104"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              We are currently stocking
              <strong>
               standard CM357
              </strong>
              with the
              <strong>
               classic pump handle
              </strong>
              , alongside the
              <strong>
               CM357a
              </strong>
              which features a more
              <strong>
               tactical magpul-esque pump!
              </strong>
              Both Variants measure in at
              <strong>
               63cm,
              </strong>
              perfect for use as
              <strong>
               both a primary
              </strong>
              or
              <strong>
               even a secondary weapon!
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Tactical Grab Bags!
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              Moving on from the usual Gun updates, this week we decided to shed some light on a piece of kit that has
              <strong>
               functional purposes both on and off the field – The Humble Grab Bag
              </strong>
              (Also known as the Tactical Man Bag) In store we carry a number of
              <strong>
               small/medium sized bags
              </strong>
              ideal for use
              <strong>
               both out and about every day
              </strong>
              or even for
              <strong>
               carrying kit out into the field!
              </strong>
              All 4 of our offerings come from
              <strong>
               Kombat UK!
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Navigation Bag:
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              Up first we have the
              <strong>
               KUK Navigation bag!
              </strong>
              Coming in around the same
              <strong>
               size as a laptop bag
              </strong>
              this tactical
              <strong>
               30L
              </strong>
              Bag can
              <strong>
               accommodate both a laptop and shed loads of kit inside!
              </strong>
              Made from
              <strong>
               600D Cordura
              </strong>
              , It is available in a
              <strong>
               number of colours: Black, OD, Coyote and BTP Camo
              </strong>
              to suit you needs, be it an everyday
              <strong>
               sleek black laptop bag
              </strong>
              or a more
              <strong>
               military Camo bag.
              </strong>
              Externally the bag features
              <strong>
               2 large utility pockets
              </strong>
              which are perfect for any small accessories such as pens, chargers, snacks or anything else you can think of. One of the outside pouches features a
              <strong>
               small ID panel
              </strong>
              alongside a
              <strong>
               huge piece of velcro real-estate
              </strong>
              to help you make this bag your own! On the other side, there is
              <strong>
               MOLLE Real estate
              </strong>
              meaning you can
              <strong>
               customize the bag even further
              </strong>
              if you need to do so. The bag also
              <strong>
               features 3! Thats right 3! carry handles
              </strong>
              alongside a
              <strong>
               padded shoulder strap
              </strong>
              making this bag easy to carry. Internally the bag features
              <strong>
               plenty of room for a laptop and note pads
              </strong>
              inside of the
              <strong>
               large internal compartment,
              </strong>
              which also features
              <strong>
               dividers
              </strong>
              to help keep all your equipment separated. Whether you’re off to a meeting, or securing some intel, the KUK Navigation Bag is a great choice!
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <strong>
               <a href="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/KUK-Nav-Bag-image-1.jpg" target="_blank">

               </a>

        <div class="art-post">
         <div class="art-post-body">
          <div class="art-post-inner art-article">
           <h2 class="art-postheader">
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96882" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to New products from Cowcow technology">
             New products from Cowcow technology
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">
            June 23rd, 2018 | Author:
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">
             News Fairy
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="art-postcontent">
            <!-- article-content -->
            <p>
             <a href="https://www.cowcowtechnology.com/" target="_blank">
              Cowcow Technology
             </a>
             have shared details of two new products:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              New product launched –
              <b>
               COWCOW Technology
              </b>
             </p>
             <p>
              We have another new items out which tailored for professional user (especially competition user). They are
              <u>
               Competition Recoil Buffer Module
              </u>
              and
              <u>
               HopUp Bucking Combo
              </u>
              .
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="https://i1.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-4.png" target="_blank">
               <img alt="image" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="218" src="https://i0.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image_thumb-4.png?resize=384%2C218" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="image" width="384"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <u>
               Competition Recoil Buffer Module
              </u>
              is produced by high quality anti-oil rubber material which is able to prevent swelling and broken and perform excellent on shock adsorption. It minimises the jamming caused during heavy usage. There are 4 levels of hardness (45°Yellow/55°Red/65°Blue/75°Black) of our buffer with 3 stainless steel spacers in a package. Users can pick your own combination (From steady soften recoil to aggressive fasten respond) with no limit to ultimate the setting. It also intended to cushion the impact of the slide against the frame, theoretically reducing the rate at which both parts become damaged from use. It is suitable for use with any 1911, and Hi-Capa 4.3/5.1 pistols and also both plastic/metal slides.
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image-5.png" target="_blank">
               <img alt="image" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="218" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/image_thumb-5.png?resize=384%2C218" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="image" width="384"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <u>
               HopUp bucking Combo
              </u>
              is manufactured by high quality anti-oil rubber material. It can prevent swelling, scratch and crash during the heavy usage. Its re-designed entrance shape can better fit with nozzle movement to prevent jamming. Flared chamber allows BB feeding much smoother. There are 3 levels of hardness (50°White/60°Red/70°Black) in a package. Those options are able to enhance different level of spin velocity (70° Low / 60° Middle / 50° High) which is suitable for different shooting environment and range. It is suitable for TM Hi-Capa, G series, M&amp;P9 &amp; M4A1 MWS.
             </p>
             <p>
              Please LIKE and FOLLOW our
              <a href="https://www.facebook.com/COWCOWTECH" target="_blank">
               Facebook Page
              </a>
              and also VISIT our
              <a href="https://www.cowcowtechnology.com" target="_blank">
               website
              </a>
              to get the latest updates.
             </p>
             <p>
              (
              <a href="https://www.cowcowtechnology.com/" target="_blank">
               Cowcow Technology
              </a>
              )
             </p>
            </blockquote>

           <h2 class="art-postheader">
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96828" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to Jia Dyi: In the name of hi-capa">
             Jia Dyi: In the name of hi-capa
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">
            June 22nd, 2018 | Author:
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">
             News Fairy
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="art-postcontent">
            <!-- article-content -->
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.jiadyi.com/" target="_blank">
              Jia Dyi
             </a>
             have been looking at race guns:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <b>
               <i>
                Jia Dyi
               </i>
              </b>
              <b>
               <i>
                ：
               </i>
              </b>
              <b>
               <i>
                In the Name of Hi-capa
               </i>
              </b>
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               Honorable Clients
              </b>
              <b>
               ：
              </b>
             </p>
             <p>
              First introduced by Marui 10 years ago and was basically modified from M1911, Hi-capa was probably the most welcomed model not only because of its capacity of
              <b>
               <i>
                double-feeding magazine
               </i>
              </b>
              , which is twice more than M1911’s 7+1 rounds, but also its
              <b>
               <i>
                various upgrade kits
               </i>
              </b>
              overwhelming consumers’ attention.
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               <i>
                Optical fiber combat sights
               </i>
              </b>
              ,
              <b>
               <i>
                light-weight construction in trigger and slide
               </i>
              </b>
              are beneficiary to rapid shot both in AIPSC race and war-game field. To increase the precision and stopping power of shots hitting on marks,
              <b>
               <i>
                extended barrel
               </i>
              </b>
              is common (thus 3.8 and 4.3 is less popular than 5.1 in race guns) to professional shooters. To compromise the weight and blow-back time issue due to long slide,
              <b>
               <i>
                split or “skeletonizing” slide
               </i>
              </b>
              is a good solution. Sometimes even a
              <b>
               <i>
                muzzle compensator
               </i>
              </b>
              is applied upon Hi-capa to shorten the time interval of sequential shots, although it is believed to be more uniqueness in appearance than practical purpose in AIPSC.
             </p>
             <p>
              Jia Dyi also provides KWC CZ75 TS replica,【
              <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JIADYI.TAIWAN/photos/a.174890159809288.1073741918.171382673493370/174890203142617/?type=3&amp;theater" target="_blank">
               KCB-89AHN
              </a>
              】,which was built a
              <b>
               <i>
                scope mount
               </i>
              </b>
              in factory settings, but it can’t match the scale to rage war against WE and KJ.
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               <i>
                “If you don’t know anything about it, it usually means money crater in front of you.”
               </i>
              </b>
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               <i>
                KJ
               </i>
              </b>
              KP-05 Hi-capa Gas blow-back pistol【
              <a href="http://www.jiadyi.com/ugC_ShowroomItem_Detail.asp?hidShowID=226" target="_blank">
               GP227
              </a>
              】
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/clip_image002-4.jpg" target="_blank">
               <img alt="clip_image002" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="246" src="https://i0.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/clip_image002_thumb-4.jpg?resize=380%2C246" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="clip_image002" width="380"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               <i>
               </i>
              </b>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             <a class="more-link" href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96828#more-96828">

             </a>

           <h2 class="art-postheader">
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96807" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to Emperion – XCORTECH: the best chronos for airsoft">
             Emperion – XCORTECH: the best chronos for airsoft
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">
            June 21st, 2018 | Author:
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">
             News Fairy
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="art-postcontent">
            <!-- article-content -->
            <p>
             <a href="http://emperionstore.com/" target="_blank">
             </a>
             <a href="http://emperionstore.com/" target="_blank">
              <img align="right" alt="unnamed" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="34" src="https://i0.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed-10.jpg?resize=200%2C34" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; float: right; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed" width="200"/>
             </a>
             Emperion have some good deals on XCORTECH chronos:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <strong>
               When you talk about FPS, Power Limit, ROF with your teammates you’re talking about Chronos. When you talk about Chronos you’re talking about XCORTECH.
              </strong>
              <br/>

           <h2 class="art-postheader">
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96774" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to Gunman Airsoft newsletter week 25 2018">
             Gunman Airsoft newsletter week 25 2018
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">
            June 20th, 2018 | Author:
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">
             News Fairy
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="art-postcontent">
            <!-- article-content -->
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.gunmanairsoft.co.uk/" target="_blank">
              <img align="right" src="https://i1.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/unnamed-3.png?w=400" style="float: right; margin: 3px; display: inline"/>
             </a>
             Here is all the latest news from
             <a href="http://www.gunmanairsoft.co.uk/" target="_blank">
              Gunman Airsoft
             </a>
             :
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              Hi, Arnies,
             </p>
             <p>
              Welcome to this week’s update from Gunman Airsoft.
             </p>
             <p>
              The FilmSim weekend at Eversley was really well attended once again, with great gameplay from everyone – thank you once again for making it another awesome weekend.  Keep your eyes on the Facebook event page for next month’s details.
             </p>
             <p>
              This weekend we still have some spaces left for the gas &amp; spring day at Tuddenham on Sunday.  You do need to pre-book as we will turn people away on the day if the spaces are filled.  Tickets can be booked up to Friday at midnight on the website and cost only £15 for a whole day of airsoft!  If there are any spaces left on the day they will be filled on a first-come-first-served basis and will cost £25, so book now to avoid disappointment.
             </p>
             <p>
              Next weekend it’s the end of the month, so it’s once again time for another exciting skirmish weekend at Tuddenham.  Places can be pre-booked online by a £15 security deposit – the remaining £10 can be paid on the day by cash, card or by presenting a valid loyalty voucher.  We strongly recommend booking as this is a popular weekend and with a bit of luck, the weather will be great!  Weekend tickets are also available, and on-site camping is free from Friday night.  If enough people want it, we may even fire up the big screen for a movie or two.
             </p>
             <p>
              <u>
              </u>
              <a href="http://mailpad.padwebsitedesign.co.uk/t/j-l-nydqiy-aillyjtt-y/" target="_blank">
               Tuddenham Calendar
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="http://mailpad.padwebsitedesign.co.uk/t/j-l-nydqiy-aillyjtt-j/" target="_blank">
               Eversley Calendar
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              (
              <a href="http://www.gunmanairsoft.co.uk/" target="_blank">
               Gunman Airsoft
              </a>
              )
             </p>
            </blockquote>

         <div class="art-post-body">
          <div class="art-post-inner art-article">
           <h2 class="art-postheader">
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/96766" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to Introducing AW Custom NE1003 &amp; NE1004 pistols">
             Introducing AW Custom NE1003 &amp; NE1004 pistols
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">
            June 19th, 2018 | Author:
            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">
             News Fairy
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="art-postcontent">
            <!-- article-content -->
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.armorerworks.com/?&amp;" target="_blank">
              AW Custom
             </a>
             have shared details of their new NE1003 &amp; NE1004 pistols:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img alt="unnamed(7)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="253" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed7-5.jpg?resize=380%2C253" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(7)" width="380"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Compact Configuration
               <br/>
              </strong>
              1911 pistol is still one of the most famous and popular pistol after a century past. The pistol compactness is the trend nowadays and hence the AW Custom™ NE10 Series Pistol in front of you.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Ported &amp; Vented
               <br/>
              </strong>
              AW Custom™ NE10 Series Pistol comes with unique ported slide and stylish vented barrel to make up of its iconic design. The ported design also benefits faster blowback cycling from recoil action.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Ergonomic Pistol Grip
               <br/>
              </strong>
              AW Custom™ knows about what our customers need and we designed the rubberized pistol grip with finger grooves for shooters to achieve a firmer grip on the pistol and quicker reloading action.
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img alt="unnamed(11)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="253" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed11-3.jpg?resize=380%2C253" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(11)" width="380"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               AW Custom™ NE1003 &amp; NE1004 Pistols
              </a>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/FiG/m/122176">
               <br/>
              </a>
              It’s already a century. 1911 Pistol is still one of the most famous and popular pistol model on earth. It’s semi-automatic mechanism is a ground-breaking innovation in the past and influenced many firearm designs in modern days.
             </p>
             <p>
              AW Custom™ NE1003 and NE1004 Pistols are the two-tone configuration models under NE10 Series. The ported slide, the vented barrel and the redesigned compact lower frame will give NE10 Series Pistol a unique and yet innovative appearance among the market.
             </p>
             <p>
              Nowadays, "Compactness" is a huge trend for gun lovers since smaller pistol can be controlled, handled and carried easily in daily life. Hence, AW Custom™ NE10 Series Pistol is now in front of you.
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img align="right" alt="unnamed(12)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="100" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed12.png?resize=99%2C100" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; float: right; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(12)" width="99"/>
              </a>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               Little But Fierce
              </a>
              <br/>
              Size doesn’t really matter. Compact configuration is a style without compensating anything from its original mechanism. AW Custom™ Tech Team ensures the NE10 Series Pistol will operate as good as our other NE Series Pistols.
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               More Detail
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img align="left" alt="unnamed(13)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="100" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed13.png?resize=99%2C100" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; float: left; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(13)" width="99"/>
              </a>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               Ported &amp; Vented Design
              </a>
              <br/>
              AW Custom™ NE10 Series Pistol comes with ported slide and vented barrel can be identified to be its iconic design. The ported slide design will also results in faster blowback cycling from its recoil action.
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               More Detail
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img align="right" alt="unnamed(14)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="100" src="https://i0.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed14.png?resize=99%2C100" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; float: right; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(14)" width="99"/>
              </a>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               Designed Ergonomically
              </a>
              <br/>
              AW Custom™ Tech Team designed a brand new rubberized pistol grip only for NE10 Series Pistol. The textured surface and the finger grooves can let shooters achieving a firmer grip on the pistol and faster magazine reloading action.
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               More Detail
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img align="left" alt="unnamed(15)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="100" src="https://i2.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed15.png?resize=99%2C100" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; float: left; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(15)" width="99"/>
              </a>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               Not Only The Pistol
              </a>
              <br/>
              Not only the slide and frame are redesigned. The NE10 Series Pistol Magazine will also become shorter in size to fit into the compact lower frame. However, the capacity of the magazine will decrease from 15 to 13 BBs.
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               More Detail
              </a>
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               <img alt="unnamed(16)" border="0" data-recalc-dims="1" height="253" src="https://i1.wp.com/arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/unnamed16-3.jpg?resize=380%2C253" style="border-top: 0px; border-right: 0px; background-image: none; border-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border-left: 0px; margin: 3px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px" title="unnamed(16)" width="380"/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/QEZ/m/122176" target="_blank">
               AW Custom™ NE10 Series Pistol
              </a>
              <a href="http://swiindustries.com/r/FiG/m/122176">
               <br/>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a name="m_-968188946902476638_techspecs">
               SPECIFICATIONS:
              </a>
             </p>
             <ul>
              <li>
               <b>
                Material:
               </b>
               Metal Alloy
              </li>
              <li>
               <b>
                Muzzle Velocity:
               </b>
               ~300FPS
              </li>
             </ul>
             <p>
              <b>
               PACKAGE INCLUDES:
              </b>
             </p>
             <ul>
              <li>
               1 x NE10 Series Pistol
              </li>
              <li>
               1 x NEMG07 Gas Magazine
              </li>
             </ul>
             <p>
              <b>
               FEATURES:
              </b>
             </p>
             <ul>
              <li>
               <p>
                Compact configuration 1911 style pistol
               </p>
              </li>
              <li>
               <p>
                Easy to control and convenient to carry
               </p>
              </li>
              <li>
               <p>
                Ported slide and vented barrel for faster and stronger recoil action
               </p>
              </li>
              <li>
               <p>
                Realistic mock firing pin mechanism
               </p>
              </li>
              <li>
               <p>
                Textured ergonomic rubber pistol grips
               </p>
              </li>
              <li>
               <p>
                Shorter magazine mechanism to fit the newly designed compact lower frame
               </p>
              </li>
             </ul>
             <p>
              (
              <a href="http://www.armorerworks.com/?&amp;" target="_blank">
               AW Custom
              </a>
              )
             </p>
            </blockquote>

             G&amp;G 2300r drum magazines
            </a>
           </h2>
           <div class="art-postheadericons art-metadata-icons">

            <a href="http://arniesairsoft.co.uk/news2/author/newsfairy" rel="author" title="Posts by News Fairy">

G-08-170 comes with a strong winding motor powered by 7.4v 800mAh battery for seamless gameplay. An on/off switch located on the rear of the drum magazine makes it easy to operate.
              <br/>
              Similar to the ARP 9 1500r Dum Magazine, the G-08-171 manual drum magazine uses the same finger grooves for fast and easy manual rotation. With an enlarged hole for bottles, pouring and reloading your drum magazine will be a breeze. Contact your local dealer for pricing and availability.
